INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM - VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-V, BLOCKS 1-12
[அரசாணை (நிலை) எண். 272, தொழில் (ஜி.ஐ.எம்)த் துறை, நாள் 13 அக்டோபர் 2021,
புரடடாசி 27, பிலவ, திருவள்ளுவர் ஆண்டு-2052.]
No.II(2)/IND/707(b-1)/2021
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the 
Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District for a public purpose, namely, in establishing 
a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 113.25.50 hectares 
in Block-1 to 12, Unit-V is under acquisition for the above said project in the Madavankurichi Village in 
Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows :
TAMIL  NADU
GOVERNMENT GAZETTE
EXTRAORDINARY	
PUBLISHED  BY  AUTHORITY
	
©	
[Regd. No. TN/CCN/467/2012-14.
GOVERNMENT  OF  TAMIL  NADU	
[R. Dis. No. 197/2009.	
	
	
	
2021	
[Price:  Rs.76.00 Paise. 
No.480]	
CHENNAI, WEDNESDAY, OCTOBER 13,  2021		
	
	
	
	
Purattasi 27, Pilava, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2052

This declaration is made under Section 19(1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project affected family in Block No.1 to 12 of Unit-V and hence 
the Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition officer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Officer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
73
FORM VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-VI, BLOCKS 1-11
[அரசாணை (நிலை) எண். 273, தொழில் (ஜி.ஐ.எம்)த் துறை, நாள் 13 அக்டோபர் 2021, புரடடாசி 27, பிலவ, திருவள்ளுவர் ஆண்டு-2052.]
No.II(2)/IND/707(b-2)/2021
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi 
District for a public purpose, namely, in establishing a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR. 
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 110.96.34 hectares in Block-1 to 11, Unit-VI is under acquisition for the above 
said project in the Madavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows:

  11.44.50
 This declaration is made under Section 19(1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project affected family in Block No.1 to 11 of Unit-VI and hence 
the Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply. 
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Land Acquisition officer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Officer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
